msg:On the positive side: The hotel itself is quite great, playground and pools were appealing, several good activities for kids, restaurant and breakfast were also very good and staff very friendly (especially in restaurant)

In the negative side: the location is not good, at least 8-10km from everything. No any restaurant or activities nearby, need to take a taxi for everything with at least 40min to 1h drive. One of the restaurant (noodle one) closed quite early so dinner in hotel was limited to 2 restaurants. In addition, because of weather (wind and a bit cold) beach was not suitable for us to stay and pools were closed. 

Good hotel for company events or short family stay (max 2 days) but not for prolonged family vacation (week)

msg:Wonderful hotel in a remote area close to Haikou. Great amenities and staff. Got upgraded to an executive room with a fantastic view for a small fee, with access to the executive lounge with complimentary drinks. 
This hotel attracts a family crowd, which means that it‚Äôs hard to find a peaceful spot. Kids are running everywhere are parents are on their phones, there‚Äôs lots of screaming, shouting and running. Shadow spots around the pool are limited, so it‚Äôs not unusual that a family will sit next to you and talk to each other very loudly. I had a hard time trying to read and concentrate with all the noise and video calls that were happening at all times. It would really help if this hotel could limit the children area from the adult area, or at least have different pools, or make some pool rules so we can all enjoy a peaceful holiday. Breakfast is also insane with all the screaming and the food-wasting with kids serving themselves. Again, an adult-only area would really help.
In any case, once you manage to escape the madness, this hotel is impressive, and the room was super comfortable. The food was of excellent quality and rich in variety. They have a complimentary shuttle bus to different parts of the city, so if you would like to have dinner outside, they also have that covered. Anyway, a Didi to anywhere is from 15-30 RMB. The staff will go the extra mile to make your stay more comfortable and enjoyable. I would recommend this hotel to families.

The room is bright and odorless. The balcony has a good view of the sea. The room service is diligent. They are polite to guests.
The whole hotel is like a seaside garden house, a step away from the beach bay. The environment is so beautiful and very quiet. The hotel has complete facilities, including a swimming pool and a children's playground. It is especially suitable for leisure and vacation, especially for parent-child travel. I will definitely bring my granddaughter to stay in this hotel this winter.
The breakfast is rich. Compared with all the other hotels I have stayed in, the most distinctive one is the Hainan-style nourishing herbal tea, including tortoise jelly, sago, coconut fruit and other Hainan-style fruit pieces with coconut milk, which are delicious and healthy. 
I especially want to praise Nita from the guest relations department. When I checked in, she took the initiative to call to ask about my experience and requirements. Her tone was sincere and kind. When I checked out, Nita called me specifically to let me give my opinions and suggestions on the hotel's services. Miss Nita's service was meticulous and thoughtful, making me feel at home. First, after checking in on the first day, I went to play the amusement facilities at night. I could only play once, which was fine. The key is that the auntie asked to check the information one by one, which gave people a feeling of anti-theft. In fact, the carousel, those children went on, didn‚Äôt they just turn, and that area is relatively remote. There is no place to eat, and usually you eat in the hotel. I feel that few outsiders go there. Then there is the swimming ring. Children must wear it when they go into the water. Other five-star hotels do charge, but generally they just charge a token fee. If you go to take it, they won‚Äôt say anything. This hotel locked it and said that it must be charged. On May Day, they took out a lot of floating boards and so on, which can be used. So those who went earlier should be treated differently?
Second, as I mentioned before, it is not very convenient to eat. You either order takeout or eat at the hotel.
Third, a double bed costs 1.2, but Ctrip says it costs 1.35. Then my child fell off the bed at night, and there were two scars on his neck and back, and the sheets were stained with blood. Because I was a platinum member, I upgraded the room type for free, so I thought, forget it. If I bring this up, it feels like I am exploiting the child. At that time, I simply disinfected it and sent the photos. Now I think that I should have taken it to the hospital for trea**ent. The service staff was very polite and asked twice. Because I was a little busy when I came back, I didn‚Äôt comment. But now I think it was actually perfunctory, because I took a photo at that time, and the wound was very obvious. When I came back, I found that the child had a scar on the wound. I don‚Äôt know what I was thinking at the time;
Fourth, the room is OK, and it is also the style I like, but, apart from the scratches from falling, I don't know if it's because we are too close to the sea, but there were so many mosquitoes at night that we couldn't sleep. The red spots on my child's back in the picture below are from the bites. I've stayed in many hotels, but this one has the most mosquitoes. I don't know why. Fifth, when I checked in, they said that I had upgraded the room type and had two breakfasts. They asked me to sign to confirm. I hesitated for a moment. I thought two breakfasts were also included. Then I signed. After I signed, they told me that they made a mistake and did not include breakfast. This is not bad. It is indeed not included. However, compared with other five-star hotels, this handling method is slightly worse. Because only the child eats breakfast, when I stayed at Marriott, I only ordered breakfast. When I checked in, they told me directly that they would give me another one. I think this is the service of a five-star hotel. I'm not trying to take advantage of it, but people are like this. If someone gives you breakfast, you will feel very comfortable and happy. Now I think that it is reasonable to ask for breakfast for the baby after making two cuts; Of course, the hotel may not be very profitable now, because I didn‚Äôt see many people on May Day.
